        if (!wb.settings.isMobileDevice && !wb.settings.disableBackground) {
            var $html = $('html'),
                $body = $('body'),
                leftBackground = '',
                rightBackground = '',
                backgroundColor = '';
            
            if (leftBackground)
                $html.css('background', leftBackground);
            if (rightBackground)
                $body.css('background', rightBackground);
            if (backgroundColor)
                $html.css('background-color', backgroundColor);
        }
    

    
        var container = $('#brandVote');
        if (container.length) {
            $.post('/favoritebrands/getvotes/' + container.data('brandId'), function (html) {
                container.html(html);
                $("h1").addClass("brand-header");
            });
        }
    

    
        var $contanier = $("#visitedGoodsContanier");
        var cssToLoad = '//static.wbstatic.net/s/NewReceipts.ascx.min.css?49d7a22eb13c7193';
        $contanier.loadVisitedGoods = function () {
            $(window).off('scroll.visited');
            $.when(wb.utils.css.require(cssToLoad)).then(function() {
                $.post("/visitedgoods", { count: $contanier.attr("data-count") }, function (html) {
                    $contanier.html(html);
                }, "html");
            });
        };      
        $(window).on('scroll.visited', function() {
            wb.utils.isElementInViewport($contanier, true) && $contanier.loadVisitedGoods();
        }).trigger('scroll.visited');
    

});
